 The Supreme Court has got three new judges
 mangalvaar ko chif justise deepak mishra ne ek parmparik samaaroh main justise indira banerjee, justise vineet saran or justise ke em joseph ko pad kii shapath dilaai
 Among these, there was a controversy over the appointment of Justice KM Joseph that seniority was not taken into consideration and he was placed third on the list, while topping the SC collegium
 aaie jaanate hai supreme court main varishthata kis tarah se tay hoti he or kya tha vivaad
 
 
 What was the controversy? First of all, what is the dispute about this? In fact, on January 10, the Collegium recommended Justice Joseph, who was the Chief Justice of Uttarakhand High Court, to be a judge of the Supreme Court
 unke alaava varisht vakil indu malhotra kaa bhi naam tha
 But in April, the government issued a warrant for Malhotra's appointment and returned Justice Joseph's name
 iske baad 16 july ko collegium ne phir justise joseph ke naam ko aage badhaayaa or unke saath do anya naam justise indira banerjee or justise vineet saran kaa naam bhi diya
 The government issued a warrant for the appointment of the three judges last week, but Justice Joseph was ranked after Justice Banerjee and Justice Saran, which means he became junior to both the judges, while for him The recommendation was made before both judges
 supreme court ke kai jajon ko lagata he ki sarkaar ne varishthata tay karne kii sthapit prakriya kaa ulanghan kiya he
 Justice Joseph was considered to be the Chief Justice, according to the most qualified Indian Express newspaper
 The Collegium had said, "justice Joseph is a senior and qualified and suitable candidate from all the judges of the High Court to become the Chief Justice of the Supreme Court in all respects
" 'supreme court main kaise varishthata tay hoti hesupreme court menshamil karne kii tithi ar shapath lene ke aadhaar par jajon kii varishthata tay kii jaati he
 That is, the judge who took the oath first was senior to the judges who took the oath later
 asal main is bare main koi nirdhaarit niyam nahin he
 It is also not clear that if many judges take oath on the same date, then how should their seniority be decided
 sarkaar iske liye warrant ek kram main jari karti he, to isamen kram ke hisaab se pehle jiskaa warrant jari hota he use shapath grahan karaayaa jaataa he
 For example, the order appointing the current Chief Justice Deepak Mishra and retired Justice j Chelameswar was of the same date, but Mishra's warrant was before Chelameswar in the order, so he took the oath first and was considered senior to Chelamescher
 isi aadhaar par vah chif justise bhi ban gaye
 The warrant for appointment of judges is issued on the basis of the recommendation of the collegium, which consists of five senior judges of the Supreme Court
 lekin warrant jari karne kaa antim nirnay sarkaar karti he
 On what basis does the collegium recommend it? It is actually an objective process, in which seniority is not taken care of
 merit ke alaava collegium yah bhi dekhtaa he ki sambandhit jaj supreme court main laane ke liye upyukt he yaa nahin
 Along with seniority, merit, care is also taken to ensure that there is balanced representation in the Supreme Court of various High Courts
 sarkaar kaa ye he tarksarkaar kaa tark he ki use teenon jajon ke naam ek hi din mili the
 According to the All India Seniority List of High Court Judges, if all the judges speak according to principle, then all three judges have the same seniority
 isamen is baat par vichaar nahin kiya jaataa ki warrant ke liye sifarish kis tithi par ai thi
 Government sources say that the judges' All India seniority is counted from the day of their appointment to the High Court
 justise indira banerjee kii hoicourt main niyukti 5 farvari 2002 ko hui thi, vineet saran kii niyukti 14 farvari 2002 tathaa justise ke
 M
 joseph ko 14 oktober 2004 ko kerala hoicourt main jaj banaaya gaya tha
 In All India seniority, Justice Banerjee is at number four, Saran at number five and Joseph at number 39
 ham jahaan kaam karte hai vahaan aise bhi kai log hote hai, jinhen ham pasand nahin karte hai

 Partial change of Supreme Court on SC-ST Act
 No need to take permission before arresting SC
 SC has partially changed its decision regarding SC-ST Act
 supreme court ne puraane faisle main kuch aanshik badlaav kiye hai
 According to the new change, now government servants and ordinary citizens will not need to get permission before arresting them
 SC / ST act ke praavdhaanon ko halkaa karne ke supreme court ke faisle ke khilaaf centre sarkaar kii punarvichaar yachika par centre sarkaar ko raahat mili he

 jo bhi he, supreme court ke is aadesh ke baad police kii javabdehi kya he, use lekar samaj to banegi, jab sarkaar hi prachaar karegi or adhikari kadam uthaane ko baadhya honge to kuch to asar hoga
 At least those fighting mob violence have a moral and legal order in support of which they can go to court and raise their voice against this trend
 bheed koi ek prakaar kii nahin hoti he
 When the 18 accused of raping an 11-year-old girl were brought to court in Chennai, the lawyers started beating them up
 police ne kisi tarah vakeelon ko roka
 Nobody is in favor of rape, but does anyone have any leeway to break up on someone with a crowd
 adaalat ke parisar ke bheetar vakeelon kaa yah vyavhaar insaaf ke lihaaz se kya sahi he? phir court kii kya zarurat he, kanoon kii kya zarurat he
 When the crowd has to decide, then what is the need of lawyers? Police were also present in large numbers at the time of the incident
 kya supreme court ke aadesh ke baad police ko alag se naitik bal kaa tonic mil jayega to aisi bheed ko kaabo kar legi
 In Jammu's Kathua case, when the police was going to the court to file the charge sheet, a mob of lawyers also tried to stop the police
 balaatkaar or hatya kii shikaar ladki ke liye saamne ai mahila vakil ko bhi kitni mushkilon kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 In February 2016, a team of lawyers cracked down on journalists in Delhi's Patiala Court
 us vakt kanhaiya ko le jaaya ja rahaa tha
 He had to arrange police to protect him from the angry mob of lawyers inside the court
 aisi naubat hi kyon ai
 Will this matter reach its end as per Supreme Court guidelines
 patiala court maamle main chargeshit ho chuki he
 There are many such instances when in the name of patriotism in the case of rape, terrorism, there is a mob of lawyers and they refuse to fight the case
 upi ke rihaai manch ke mohammad shoeb se puuchhie jab ve aatank ke aarope main pakade gaye 14 ladakon ke khilaaf cese ladane gaye to upi kii kitni adaalaton main vakeelon ne hi unhen peeta, maar-markar zakhmi kar diya
 Had Mohammad Shoaib not taken the risk, the 14 boys would not have been acquitted
 khud supreme court ne na jane kitne ladke 20-20 saal aatank ke aarope main sazaa kaatane ke baad bari hue hai
 So will the mob of lawyers decide before the hearing? bheed ke kai pahalu hai
 If the crowd decides that no one will get a lawyer and they too are drawn to the violence in the court premises, then it is also against the basic concept of justice
 bharat main pichley saadhe chaar saal main bheed kii hinsa ke kai maamle hue magar kisi bhi maamle main abhi tak sazaa mukammal nahin hui he
 The Supreme Court has clearly stated that mobility will not be tolerated
 kai baar peedit behad garib hote hai isliye supreme court ne is baat kaa bhi dhyaan rakhaa he
 It has said in its guidelines that the government will pay the expenses of the victim's lawyer
 supreme court ne kaha he ki sansad kanoon banaae
 Tasheen Poonawala, the petitioner in this case, has said that he has also prepared a framework of law at his level to overcome the crowd, which is named Mashuka
 unhone kaha he ki ve jald hi iskaa praaroop kanoon mantri ravishankar prasad ko saunp denge
 This format has been introduced in Parliament by Shashi Tharoor as a private bill
 tippaniyan i wish the Supreme Court's guidelines would also be about the news channels where on a different day, there is a debate on hindu-muslim topics
 channelon par aisi baaten likhi jaati hai jinke tevar sampradayik hote hai

 bheed kaa nirmaan channelon ke zarie bhi ho rahaa he

 janata kya kya maang rahi he

 When the channels are engaged in rioting the audience through Hindu Muslim debate, then the public has started becoming a reporter on their own to address their problems
 baccha chori or gauraksha ke naam par udne vaali afvaahon or bheed ke banane kii pravriti main khaas antar nahin he
